# DOC TRIAGE - 2026-07-16

A 29-lane swarm classified every file in docs/ (incl. deos, reference, MANUAL, guides, ops) and site/ against the code at HEAD - content-vs-code, since the relicense flattened git dates. Each STALE entry lists the specific claims that no longer hold, with code refs. Both failure directions were hunted: over-pessimism (doc says blocked/planned; code shows landed) and over-claim (doc says closed/live; code shows fixture/unwired).

Tally: {'HISTORICAL': 70, 'STALE': 166, 'CURRENT': 208, 'SUPERSEDED': 11} of 455 files.

HORIZONLOG was audited separately (entry-level verdicts, no rewrites); the sweep proposal is a separate reviewable file.


## STALE (166)

### `docs/ALG-COMPLEXITY-AUDIT.md`
Dated (2026-07-08) master board of the complexity sweep. Mixed at HEAD: most Tier-2 cheap wins landed and Tier-1 #1 was closed by a different (better) mechanism, while Tier-1 #2 (FullForestAuth.lean:481 revoked.contains) and #3 (exec-lean/src/lean_apply.rs:1148 template.clone) genuinely remain. The board's per-row statuses and PLAN section are wrong in both directions and worth annotating.
- **claim:** Tier-2 #5: has_equivocation_in_past unmemoized (O(waves·P·N²)/poll), fix = precompute equivocator set — listed as an open cheap win
  **truth:** Landed: ordering.rs now documents 'The old has_equivocation_in_past rebuilt an observer's whole causal past' and uses the precomputed visible-equivocator formulation `[blocklace/src/ordering.rs:165]`
- **claim:** Tier-2 #8: coord budget `debits: Vec` as anti-replay set, O(n²)/session — open cheap win
  **truth:** Landed: `debit_set: HashSet<DebitDigest>` is the O(1) anti-replay membership twin, rebuilt from `debits` on deserialize `[coord/src/budget.rs:96]`
- **claim:** Tier-2 #10: linear `position` on SORTED `sorted_leaves` in heap_root.rs/cap_root.rs — open trivial win
  **truth:** Landed: `position_of` is a `binary_search_by` ('O(log n) vs the former O(n) scan') and range lookups use `partition_point`; cap_root.rs:528 likewise `[circuit/src/heap_root.rs:315]`
- **claim:** Tier-1 #1: nullifier double-spend gate `nf ∈ k.nullifiers` — fix = 'HashSet twin in kernel state', a pending needs-design batch
  **truth:** Closed by a different deployed mechanism: the sorted-Merkle nullifier accumulator (kernel carries `nullifierRoot`, the Poseidon2 sorted-tree root; the deployed noteSpendVmDescriptor2R24 forces freshness) — the List-scan/HashSet-twin framing is obsolete `[metatheory/Dregg2/Exec/RecordKernel.lean:433]`

### `docs/BUILD-LEAN-LINKED-NODE.md`
The operational guide's recipe, seeding flow, warm-.lake path, and toolchain pin (v4.30.0) all verify, and bootstrap.sh / seed-dregg2-closure.sh / the DREGG_REQUIRE_LEAN gate exist. But the guard section is over-pessimistic about its own defenses: the startup tripwire and the release-build default were both hardened past what the doc describes.
- **claim:** Startup — the marshal-only tripwire (node/src/main.rs): unconditionally, before any role logic, the node logs a loud `error!` if lean_available() is false (log-and-continue)
  **truth:** The tripwire lives in node/src/lib.rs and is fail-CLOSED: ANY node (solo or full) refuses to start (exit(1)) when the verified executor is not linked, unless DREGG_ALLOW_UNVERIFIED_CONSENSUS=1; the code comment explicitly says 'Historically this tripwire was LOG-ONLY' `[node/src/lib.rs:845]`
- **claim:** At runtime the node itself reports it: a marshal-only binary logs `MARSHAL-ONLY BUILD DETECTED …` at error level on startup
  **truth:** A marshal-only binary no longer runs by default — it logs REFUSING TO START and exits 1; only the explicit override path proceeds, logging 'MARSHAL-ONLY BUILD OVERRIDDEN' `[node/src/lib.rs:879-899]`
- **claim:** DREGG_REQUIRE_LEAN: 'Set it in every distribution / CI / validator build. Unset (the default) preserves warn-and-degrade for dev boxes and the non-linkable targets.'
  **truth:** The gate now has a RELEASE-DEFAULT tier: any --release build on a native archive-linkable target defaults the fail-loud gate ON (require_lean_native); the opt-out is DREGG_REQUIRE_LEAN=0. Only debug/dev builds keep warn-and-degrade by default `[dregg-lean-ffi/build.rs:1418-1441]`

### `docs/CONTENT-AND-ASSET-SPEC.md`
The spwashi task spec's Track B/C grounding still holds (spween compiler, procgen tables, and E4 /gallery publish-scene is genuinely still an unbuilt named seam — gallery publish remains procgen-only, dreggnet-quest names the flywheel as a seam). But the Track A picture is over-pessimistic: enablements E1-E3 all shipped and the 'totally greenfield visual layer' premise is false at HEAD.
- **claim:** The visual layer is totally greenfield — a grep for canvas|svg|sprite across extension/, dreggnet-web, deos-view finds zero source hits; today's richest visual is an emoji glyph
  **truth:** A full deterministic sprite pipeline ships: the dreggnet-sprite crate (AssetId → 128×128 SVG), wasm spriteSvg/traitsJson bindings, the extension's in-tab SPRITE ENGINE with the <dregg-sprite> element, and dreggnet-web's /sprite routes + gallery `[extension/src/port.ts:2452]`
- **claim:** E1 (a trait field on the asset) is an enablement to build — '(gap: zero trait fields today.)'
  **truth:** dreggnet-asset carries a committed trait root: mint_with_traits/mint_soulbound_with_traits commit an explicit root, AssetWorld::trait_root_of reads it, and the sprite/gear layer draws deterministic traits from it `[dreggnet-asset/src/lib.rs:570]`
- **claim:** E2 (a first-class weighted draw) is to-build — 'today weighting is done by repeated table slots … impractical for 1/1000'
  **truth:** DrawStream::weighted exists: a provably-fair weighted selection over a committed weight table, one draw per index `[dice/src/draw.rs:158]`
- **claim:** E3 (a traitsJson wasm getter + a <dregg-sprite> custom element) is an enablement we build first
  **truth:** Both shipped: wasm exports traitsJson (bindings_sprite.rs) and the extension registers the <dregg-sprite> element fed by the background SpriteEngine `[wasm/src/bindings_sprite.rs:139]`

  **truth:** The real full-byte MlDsaSignReal.signCore is deployed behind MlDsaKey::sign via install_lean_sign_core_real; node/tests/mldsa_live_sign.rs is the running-binary gate ('the fips204 crate leaves the node's SIGN TCB') `[node/tests/mldsa_live_sign.rs:1]`

  **truth:** BRICK K5 landed: the deployed hybrid initiator routes ML-KEM-768 encapsulation through the Lean MlKemEncaps.mlkemEncaps core (install_mlkem_verified_encaps_core wired in node/src/lib.rs; crate .encapsulate is fallback-only), gated by node/tests/mlkem_live_encaps.rs `[node/tests/mlkem_live_encaps.rs:1]`

  **truth:** Resolved: the working tree is on main (mlkem-route remains only as a stale local branch); the section is a transient note that no longer describes the tree `[git: HEAD=main, branch mlkem-route exists]`

Consistent with launch-readiness ground truth there is still no durable public deployment — but the specific blockers this plan names are gone.
- **claim:** 'The one blocker: dreggnet-web is a LIBRARY with no server bin' (HONEST BLOCKERS #1, [IN FLIGHT])
  **truth:** The server bin exists: dreggnet-web/src/bin/dreggnet-web-server.rs with a [[bin]] target, and deploy/games/dregg-web-games.service runs it (the hbox games deploy) `[dreggnet-web/Cargo.toml:28-30]`
- **claim:** Phase 3: 'the fold is NOT yet GPU-accelerated — it routes through prove_turn_chain_recursive's CPU recursion config'; wiring GPU into the fold's per-layer aggregation is a named future circuit-prove change
  **truth:** The wiring landed: ivc_turn_chain.rs (home of prove_turn_chain_recursive) imports and uses gpu_backend::prove_recursion_layer_auto_with_expose / prove_recursion_aggregation_auto_with_expose — per-layer fold proving auto-dispatches to the GPU backend (the 25x prod-wired prover) `[circuit-prove/src/ivc_turn_chain.rs:214]`
- **claim:** Phase 2 rides 'gated deploy/rollback (deploy/aws)' and key files include deploy/aws/
  **truth:** deploy/aws is superseded wholesale (content moved under deploy/aws/SUPERSEDED/); the live deploy docs are deploy/PRACTICES.md and deploy/games/ `[deploy/aws/SUPERSEDED]`
- **claim:** HONEST BLOCKERS #6: 'no dedicated games-web ops runbook'
  **truth:** Dedicated runbooks exist: deploy/games/RUNBOOK.md and deploy/games/RUNBOOK-FUNNEL.md `[deploy/games/RUNBOOK.md:1]`

### `docs/DESIGN-combat-engine.md`
A 920-line 'Status: proposed' design for world-resolved tactical combat in attested-dm. Its claims about the existing surface verify (GameAction::Attack/Use at game.rs:84-97, CombatEnemy at :434). But its premise has been overtaken: a multi-combatant tactical encounter engine shipped in attested-dm via a much simpler design that satisfies the doc's core principle (the world resolves, the AI only narrates) without any of this doc's API — resolve_combat_command, CombatRuleset, CombatState, CombatPhase, and draw manifests appear nowhere in the tree. The doc needs a status note reconciling it with the shipped engine (implemented-differently vs still-future phases like zones/rulesets-as-content).
- **claim:** Status: proposed — an additive combat subsystem for attested-dm (implying no tactical multi-combatant engine exists; 'Initial versions do not attempt…')
  **truth:** attested-dm ships a turn-based, initiative-ordered tactical encounter engine at HEAD: Combatant/EncounterRule with strike/guard/cooldown-special abilities, deterministic foe AI folded into receipted turns, dregg-dice domain-separated draws, replay-verified (examples/combat.rs drives it end-to-end) — built without this design's resolve_combat_command/CombatRuleset API `[attested-dm/src/game.rs:804]`

### `docs/DESIGN-crown-lowering-and-assurance-ladder.md`
Design/coordination artifact for the range/comparison lowering gadget + assurance ladder. The core gap it coordinates around has since been closed: the standalone gadget crate exists (constraint-lowering, including multilimb u64 borrow-chain variants beyond the design) and game-turn-slice grew its own compiler that lowers every ordering tooth through a range gadget. The TEE rung (CiAssurance::TeeAttested) remains unbuilt as the doc says. Also in tension with architectural law #1, now a CI ratchet (circuit-prove/tests/law1_enforcement_gate.rs) that forbids new Rust-authored constraints for deployed circuits and lists lean_lookup_air.rs as 'the proven range gadget' — the doc's Rust-emission route is no longer the sanctioned path to the crown.
- **claim:** Sequencing step 2 'Build emit_ge / lower_ordering_tooth standalone + unit-test it' is presented as future work to align teams on.
  **truth:** The crate exists: constraint-lowering/src/lib.rs implements emit_ge, emit_le, emit_ge_const, ColAlloc, plus emit_ge_multilimb / emit_ge_const_multilimb (multi-limb borrow chains the design never specified). `[constraint-lowering/src/lib.rs:1]`
- **claim:** "Ordering teeth — FieldGte, FieldLte, Monotonic, StrictMonotonic — ... Each is reached only by a hand-authored bit-decomposition per rule."
  **truth:** game-turn-slice now has a compiler module that lowers every ordering tooth through a reusable bit-decomposition range gadget (its lib.rs header: 'lowers every ordering tooth through a real bit-decomposition RANGE GADGET'), driven end-to-end by tests/game_program_compiler.rs. `[game-turn-slice/src/lib.rs:24]`
- **claim:** "ConstraintExpr today is Equality / Multiplication / Binary / PiBinding / Transition / Polynomial / Gated" — seven variants, nothing else.
  **truth:** ConstraintExpr at HEAD also has InvertedGated, Squared, Hash, ConditionalNonzero, AtLeastOne, Hash2to1, Hash4to1, Hash3Cap, MerkleHash8, MerkleHash, and Lookup (table membership usable for range checks). Still no native comparison variant, but the variant inventory the design reasons from is far out of date. `[circuit/src/dsl/circuit.rs:125]`

### `docs/DESIGN-dregg-dice.md`
Design spec for verifiable game randomness. The crate landed at dice/ (package name dregg-dice) and went far past the 'first slice' — but it also DIVERGED from this doc's normative protocol choices, so the doc no longer describes the shipped wire format. Over-pessimism (VRF/beacon/Hybrid all real) and normative drift (mapping algorithm, EventId derivation, API shapes) both present.
- **claim:** "The first implementation slice deliberately uses a deterministic mock or commit-reveal source ... explicitly does not implement a VRF algorithm, beacon networking, beacon proof verification, wall-clock timeout policy, or the production Hybrid."
  **truth:** dice/ implements the real post-quantum LB-VRF ServerVrf (pqvrf), a real threshold DrandBeacon (BLS pairing check), HashChainBeacon, a genesis-committed KeyChain, and Hybrid with timeout finalization — the full production endpoint, not the first slice. `[dice/src/lib.rs:17]`
- **claim:** "V1 uses deterministic rejection sampling over consecutive 64-bit words ... The simple algorithm above is normative for the first slice."
  **truth:** The shipped mapping is a fixed-width, reject-free wide multiply-and-shift (Lemire without the rejection step), and the crate explicitly says 'never data-dependent rejection sampling' — the opposite of this doc's normative algorithm. `[dice/src/draw.rs:102]`
- **claim:** EventId::derive(game_id, parent_receipt_hash, action_commitment, event_ordinal); SourceBinding/SourceEvidence enums; RandomnessSuite::V1Blake3 — 'the signatures below define the intended public surface'.
  **truth:** The shipped EventId::derive binds (game_binding, seq, pre_state_root, action_hash, event_kind, draw_count) — different fields, no event_ordinal/parent_receipt_hash — and the source/evidence types differ (Deterministic/CommitReveal/MockBeacon/ServerVrf/Hybrid with their own shapes). `[dice/src/event.rs:35]`

### `docs/DESIGN-verifiable-game.md`
The attested-dm verifiable-game roadmap. Its architecture and design laws remain the governing frame, but its 'current state' boundaries and several roadmap phases have been overtaken: replay verification exists, Phase-2 randomness landed (dice/), overworld exists (Phase 5 partially), and the STARK-soundness-is-assumed caveat is outdated. Boundary 1 (fixture attestation authenticity leg) is still true (AuthenticPolicy::AllowFixture, attested-dm/src/lib.rs:87).
- **claim:** "Current verification authenticates recorded history but does not replay resolve_action. It proves that history was not altered after recording, not that every recorded effect followed the rules."
  **truth:** GameSession::verify_replay exists and is the re-execution tier — every recorded effect is re-derived by re-running resolve_action; the overworld gates hosted travel on it. `[attested-dm/src/overworld.rs:21]`
- **claim:** "ultimate STARK soundness remains an assumption rather than a discharged proof."
  **truth:** The linking tower is complete: DeployedTraceExtract is DERIVED from the proven FRI keystone (deployedTraceExtract_of_embedding, #assert_axioms-clean) and StarkSound is a proven reduction to RSProximityCore, not an opaque assumption. `[metatheory/Dregg2/Circuit/DeployedTraceExtract.lean:176]`
- **claim:** Phase 2 ('Non-grindable randomness': VRF key registration, beacon verification, timeout receipts) is a future roadmap phase.
  **truth:** dregg-dice implements the recommended hybrid (real PQ LB-VRF + verified schedule-bound beacon + timeout finalization) and randomness evidence rides the attested-dm receipt chain, re-verified by verify_replay (attested-dm/src/game.rs:742). `[dice/src/lib.rs:17]`

### `docs/DESIGN-verified-layout-optimizer.md`
The verified allocator + optimizer design ('the snarky we never finished'). Phases 1-2 have LANDED: RotatedLayout.lean is the constructor-invariant verified allocator (Nodup disjointness, the rotated178 instance) and RotatedLayoutBridge.lean wires the emit to derive from it — the doc still presents these as the plan. The honest-floor section is also outdated: StarkSound is now a proven reduction and DeployedTraceExtract is derived from FRI math. Phase 3 (the translation-validation optimizer) remains unbuilt design, so the doc is not wholesale superseded.
- **claim:** "the disjointness invariant ('no two things write the same limb' ...) is NOT machine-checked anywhere; it is held by a comment" and Phase 1 (RotatedLayout) / Phase 2 (producer derivation) are proposed future phases.
  **truth:** metatheory/Dregg2/Circuit/Emit/RotatedLayout.lean exists: RotatedLayout carries the invariants as constructor obligations, rotated178 is the current geometry as an instance, and RotatedLayoutBridge.lean does the Phase-2 wiring so producer/circuit/emit read one source. `[metatheory/Dregg2/Circuit/Emit/RotatedLayout.lean:1]`
- **claim:** "AIR soundness is ASSUMED via the StarkSound class, reduced (not eliminated) to two named residuals (DeployedTraceExtract ... + DeployedRefines ...)" — the floor stays assumed.
  **truth:** StarkSoundReduction.lean proves starkSound_of_core (RSProximityCore → StarkSound, #assert_axioms-clean), and DeployedTraceExtract itself is DERIVED from the proven FRI keystone (deployedTraceExtract_of_embedding) — the floor is substantially discharged, not merely reduced-and-assumed. `[metatheory/Dregg2/Circuit/StarkSoundReduction.lean:1]`

Its top-ranked recommendations have since LANDED, so its recorded current-state is over-pessimistic on all three headline gaps: the epoch manifest/handshake exists (dregg-epoch), the multichain treasury view exists (TreasuryView), and the treasury is now wired into the live bot's PayState. - **claim:** "directly answers 'how does a client know its epoch?' (today: no answer)" — the epoch manifest + handshake is recommendation #1, unbuilt.
  **truth:** The dregg-epoch crate implements exactly this: EpochManifest derived from the real baked constants (V3_STAGED_REGISTRY_FP, descriptor set, caveat tags) + check_compatibility returning a typed EpochCompat verdict; only the transport wire remains a named seam. `[dregg-epoch/src/lib.rs:1]`
- **claim:** "The treasury is Solana-only today ... built but NOT joined into the live bot (PayState has ledger+watcher, no Treasury/Sweeper — built+tested, unwired)" and ProvenForeignHolding "feeds governance voting weight, not the treasury".
  **truth:** PayState now routes every detected payment through Treasury::record_payment backed by a persistent SqliteTreasuryStore, and the non-custodial multichain TreasuryView points the ProvenForeignHolding facts at the treasury's own addresses across Solana/Base/Cosmos (with a driving test dregg-interchain-gov/tests/multichain_treasury_view.rs). `[discord-bot/src/pay.rs:242]`
- **claim:** Recommendation #1 (cross-chain treasury): "Treasury needs per-chain holding fields + a verifier hook" — pending.
  **truth:** dregg-pay/src/multichain.rs implements TreasuryView with declared TreasurySlots, consensus-proof-gated counting, and rejection of unproven/foreign-address facts — the recommended 'small wire' is built. `[dregg-pay/src/multichain.rs:1]`

### `docs/FINDING-checkpoint-pipeline-unwired.md`

### `docs/ONBOARDING.md`
Orientation doc; every referenced path exists (OVERVIEW.md, atlas/atlas.html, CONSTRUCTIVE-KNOWLEDGE.md, DREGG-CALCULUS.md, CLAIMS.md, reference/, QUICKSTART.md, guide/, MANUAL/, sdk-py). - **claim:** 'Every state transition is gated by an unforgeable capability, leaves a verifiable receipt, and carries a STARK proof a light client can check without re-running history.'
  **truth:** Per-turn STARK proving on the node is opt-in and OFF by default: it must be enabled with --prove-turns / DREGG_PROVE_TURNS=1 (devnet). By default committed turns do not carry proofs — proving is off the commit path. The capability gate and receipt clauses hold; the blanket carries-a-STARK-proof clause describes the opt-in mode as if it were universal. `[node/src/blocklace_sync.rs:4768; node/src/lib.rs:1464-1466]`

### `docs/OPERATOR-ONBOARDING.md`
The three-verb operator dance (gen-validator-key / add-validator / join) matches node/src/operator_join.rs, and the quorum table matches quorum_threshold. But the identity model predates the PQ hybrid: the doc describes the committee and federation_id in Ed25519-only terms, while genesis at HEAD commits the id to the hybrid (Ed25519 + ML-DSA-65) roster.
- **claim:** 'A federation is a fixed committee of validator Ed25519 public keys. The federation_id is ... derive_federation_id_with_epoch(sorted_committee_pubkeys, committee_epoch)' — presented as THE derivation every node agrees on.
  **truth:** Genesis derives the federation_id from the sorted committee HYBRID member ids (hybrid_id_commitment(ed25519, ml_dsa) per validator) via derive_federation_id_hybrid_with_epoch, 'so the id commits to the ML-DSA roster, not Ed25519 alone.' The doc's ed-only derivation matches only the add-validator reroll path (operator_join.rs:177), which now diverges from what a hybrid genesis writes — a code seam the doc's 'the exact derivation the node uses' claim papers over. `[node/src/genesis.rs:95-99 (GenesisConfig.federation_id doc), :146-148; federation/src/identity.rs:65; contrast node/src/operator_join.rs:177]`

  **truth:** Full-turn STARK proving on the node commit path is gated by full_turn_proving_enabled, which defaults to false; the proof is attached only when the operator enables it. ### `docs/deos/TRUSTLESS-SOLANA-BRIDGE.md`
Passes 1-4 are real and verified in code (derive_stake_table, rotate, effective_stake + StakeHistory sysvar, PohAnchorPolicy, mint_against_lock_proof_anchored, and the 2026-07-12 bare-table test-gating all exist). But the closing 'Honest status' over-claims: it asserts no consensus-soundness item remains and only the Option-B optimization stands between HEAD and a COMPLETE trustless bridge, while three code-visible soundness suspects on exactly this path are open and triage-flagged in the repo's own record.
- **claim:** "the bridge is now trustless modulo the weak-subjectivity anchor (plus the named stake-timing / lock-layout / bank-hash-version refinements above, none of which is a consensus-soundness hole)" and "the honest distance to a fully-COMPLETE trustless Solana bridge is now a single optimization, not a soundness item".
  **truth:** Three open soundness suspects live on this exact path (codex-flagged, HORIZONLOG P1 'CLOSE VALUE-PATH HOLES'): (1) rotation admits the next epoch's table via plain verify_supermajority WITHOUT the authorized-voter binding tally_authorized provides — the doc-comment at rotate() says so explicitly; (2) derive_stake_table proves supplied accounts' inclusion but nothing proves stake-set COMPLETENESS, so omitting stake accounts shrinks the denominator and lets a minority clear 'supermajority' in rotated epochs; (3) the verified relation is an exact-slot ≥2/3 vote (closer to optimistic confirmation than rooted finality) while ConsensusEvidence.slot is documented as 'finalized'. `[bridge/src/solana_provenance.rs:697-726]`
- **claim:** derive_stake_table means the EpochStakeTable is 'proven from the bank hash the votes attest, not supplied as trusted input' — presented as closing the stake-provenance trust gap.
  **truth:** derive_stake_table verifies inclusion of each SUPPLIED stake/vote account and sums only those; there is no completeness floor (e.g. cross-check against the StakeHistory sysvar total), so the relayer chooses which stake accounts exist — sound at the pinned anchor epoch (root equality pins the full table) but not through rotation. `[bridge/src/solana_provenance.rs:457-527]`
- **claim:** ConsensusEvidence describes 'the Solana slot the lock was finalized in' / the doc speaks of verifying finality.
  **truth:** The struct's own field doc says 'finalized' but the verification checks an exact-slot stake-weighted vote (no lockout/root history — the wire parser takes only the newest slot/hash from Vote/TowerSync), i.e. optimistic-confirmation semantics, not rooted finality. `[bridge/src/solana_trustless.rs:69-75]`

  **truth:** The wake still rides EmitEvent, but the notify authority is no longer merely 'designed and held': each SwarmMember carries a dregg_firmament::NotifyCap whose badge_mask is enforced on every wake via NotifyCap::signal_admissible, the Rust mirror of the verified Dregg2.Firmament.NotifyAuthority.NotifyCap.signalAdmissible. `[starbridge-v2/src/swarm.rs:94]`

### `docs/reference/MASK-RECON-WRAP-INVESTIGATION.md`
Investigation asserts a REAL, live capability-authorization forgery in the deployed cap-open circuit (32-bit maskRecon binds only mod p; a cap granting nothing authorizes a transfer), verdict '(A) confirmed live, not undeterminable'. The doc lacks the resolution banner its sibling WRAP-CLASS-AUDIT carries, so it still reads as an open live hole.

  **truth:** capOpenConstraintsEff now emits maskReconLoGate + maskReconHiGate (per-16-bit-limb reconstruction, each sum < 2^16 < p) and maskReconGate_of_limbs DERIVES the full 32-bit recon; CapOpenRowCanon carries only genuine cell canonicality, reconExact is discharged. Header comment labels this 'the MASK-RECON-WRAP FIX'. `[metatheory/Dregg2/Circuit/Emit/CapOpenEmit.lean:266-286 (maskReconLoGate/HiGate in list); metatheory/Dregg2/Circuit/DeployedCapOpen.lean:448-459 (maskReconGate_of_limbs discharge)]`

  **truth:** Only two proc-macro attributes exist (dregg_caveat at lib.rs:80, dregg_effect at lib.rs:142); the dregg_circuit macro is gone — the crate header says the hand-rolled dregg_circuit STARK engine was removed `[dregg-dsl/src/lib.rs:13-15]`
- **claim:** A #[dregg_caveat]/#[dregg_effect] macro expands into eight code generators including emit_stark (emit_stark_impl.rs, {Name}Circuit compile-time STARK AIR)
  **truth:** SEVEN backends; the former emit_stark backend has been removed along with that engine; native Plonky3 (gen_plonky3) is the proving backend — there is no emit_stark_impl.rs in dregg-dsl/src/ `[dregg-dsl/src/lib.rs:3-15]`
- **claim:** emit_stark is exercised separately by dregg-dsl-tests prove/verify tests; range checks compile to bit-decomposition in both emit_stark and gen_plonky3
  **truth:** emit_stark no longer exists; the range-check soundness note in the crate now names gen_plonky3 only `[dregg-dsl/src/lib.rs:37-43]`
- **claim:** There are 21 directories under starbridge-apps/ (incl. shared/)
  **truth:** There are 31 directories under starbridge-apps/ (32 entries including README.md) — the app roster grew (agent-orchestration, branch-stitch-multiplayer, execution-lease, org, vat, billing, guard, domains, edge-mandate, tussle, kvstore, etc.) `[starbridge-apps/ (ls: 31 dirs)]`
- **claim:** The doc omits the differential harness's own caveat that plonky3_runner never instantiates the macro-emitted {Name}P3Air (agreement is against a re-derived mirror)
  **truth:** The crate header flags this as the CURRENT RESOLUTION of the gen_plonky3 vote — driving the emitted {Name}P3Air through prove/verify remains an open seam the doc's cross-validation section over-claims past `[dregg-dsl/src/lib.rs:25-35]`
